6932: const calcRecentSpendShare = (rows = [], item = {}, endDateStr = "", windowDays = 7) => {
6933:   const endDate = toDateOnly(endDateStr || getLatestDateFromRows(rows));
6934:   const totalSpend = safeNum(item.spend || rows.reduce((s, r) => s + safeNum(r.spend), 0));
6935:   if (!rows.length || !endDate || totalSpend <= 0) return 0;
6936:   const lookbackDays = Math.max(1, Math.min(7, windowDays));
6937:   const cutoff = new Date(endDate.getTime() - (lookbackDays - 1) * ATTRIBUTION_DAY_MS);
6938:   const recentSpend = rows.reduce((s, r) => {
6939:     const d = toDateOnly(r.date);
6940:     if (!d || d < cutoff || d > endDate) return s;
6941:     return s + safeNum(r.spend);
6942:   }, 0);
6943:   return clamp(recentSpend / totalSpend, 0, 1);
6944: };

6946: const getEventAttributionProfile = (item = {}) => {
6947:   const enabled = Boolean($("eventProtectionToggle")?.checked);
6948:   const rows = Array.isArray(item.rows) ? item.rows : [];
6949:   const adProducts = new Set();
6950:   if (item.adProduct) adProducts.add(item.adProduct);
6951:   if (Array.isArray(item.adProducts)) item.adProducts.forEach(x => adProducts.add(x));

6959:   const todayUtc = new Date(Date.UTC(today.getFullYear(), today.getMonth(), today.getDate()));

6994:   }

7014: const getDecisionConfidence = () => getNumericInput("decisionConfidence",0.90,0.50,0.99);
7015: const getMinStableDays = () => Math.round(getNumericInput("minStableDays",2,1,14));
7016: const getBayesianCvrStats = (item = {}, globalMetrics = null) => {
7017:   const g=globalMetrics||sumMetrics(AdsStore.view||[]), clicks=Math.max(0,safeNum(item.clicks)), orders=Math.max(0,Math.min(clicks,safeNum(item.orders)));
7018:   const priorMean=clamp(g.cvr||0.05,0.005,0.30), strength=24;
7019:   const a=priorMean*strength+orders, b=(1-priorMean)*strength+Math.max(0,clicks-orders), mean=a/(a+b);
7020:   const variance=(a*b)/(((a+b)**2)*(a+b+1)), sd=Math.sqrt(Math.max(0,variance));
7021:   const conf=getDecisionConfidence(), z=conf>=0.95?1.96:conf>=0.90?1.645:1.44;
7022:   const lower=clamp(mean-z*sd,0,1), upper=clamp(mean+z*sd,0,1);
7023:   const zeroOrderClicks=Math.ceil(Math.log(1-conf)/Math.log(Math.max(0.001,1-priorMean)));
7024:   return {priorMean,strength,mean,lower,upper,zeroOrderClicks,confidence:conf};
7025: };
7026: const getAdaptiveDecisionThresholds = (item = {}, targetAcos = null, globalMetrics = null) => {
7027:   const g=globalMetrics||sumMetrics(AdsStore.view||[]), stats=getBayesianCvrStats(item,g);
7028:   const aov=item.orders>0?item.sales/item.orders:(g.orders>0?g.sales/g.orders:15),targetReady=Number.isFinite(targetAcos)&&targetAcos>.005,targetCpa=targetReady?Math.max(1,aov*targetAcos):null,mismatch=getBidRiskProfile(item.name||item.searchTerm||item.targeting||"").hardMismatch;
7029:   const clickThreshold=Math.max(8,Math.ceil(stats.zeroOrderClicks*(mismatch?0.60:1.00)));
7030:   const spendThreshold=targetCpa!==null?Math.max(5,targetCpa*(mismatch?0.65:1.15)):0;
7031:   return {stats,aov,targetAcos:targetReady?targetAcos:null,targetReady,targetCpa,clickThreshold,spendThreshold};
7032: };

5487: const getAdProductMeta = (code) => AMAZON_AD_PRODUCT_META[String(code || "SP").toUpperCase()] || AMAZON_AD_PRODUCT_META.SP;
5488: const getAdProductDisplayLabel = (code) => getAdProductMeta(code).label;

5490: const isBulkAllowedAdProduct = (code) => Boolean(getAdProductMeta(code).bulkAllowed);
5491: const detectAttributionWindowFromHeader = (header = [], fallbackCode = "SP") => {
5492:   const joined = header.map(cleanHeaderCompact).join("|");
5493:   if (/14(day|天)|14d/.test(joined)) return 14;
5494:   if (/7(day|天)|7d/.test(joined)) return 7;
5495:   const advertiserType = $("advertiserType")?.value || "seller";
5496:   if (String(fallbackCode || "SP").toUpperCase() === "SP" && advertiserType === "vendor") return 14;
5497:   return getAdProductMeta(fallbackCode).defaultAttributionDays || 7;

5499: const buildReportSchemaAudit = (reportType, header = [], map = {}, rows = [], fileName = "") => {
5500:   const warnings = [];
5501:   const requiredByType = {
5502:     ADS_REPORT: ["date", "campaign", "impr", "clicks", "spend", "sales7d", "orders7d"],
5503:     BUSINESS_REPORT: ["asin", "sessions", "units", "sales"],
5504:     PLACEMENT_REPORT: ["campaign", "placement", "impr", "clicks", "spend"],
5505:     SQP_REPORT: ["query", "searchVolume", "imprShare", "clickShare", "purchShare"],
5506:     TRANSACTION_REPORT: ["postedAt", "type", "productSales", "sellingFees", "fbaFees", "total", "status"]
5507:   };
5508:   const required = requiredByType[reportType] || [];
5509:   const missing = required.filter(k => !map[k]);
5510:   if (missing.length) warnings.push(`Missing columns: ${missing.join(", ")}`);
5511:   const adProduct = map.adProductType || (reportType === "ADS_REPORT" ? detectAdProduct(header, rows, map.adProduct) : "");
5512:   const attributionWindowDays = reportType === "ADS_REPORT" || reportType === "PLACEMENT_REPORT" ? detectAttributionWindowFromHeader(header, adProduct || "SP") : null;
5513:   if (reportType === "ADS_REPORT" && adProduct !== "SP") warnings.push(`${getAdProductDisplayLabel(adProduct)} imported as analysis-only; SP Bulk export is blocked for this report type.`);
5514:   if (reportType === "SQP_REPORT") warnings.push("SQP is search funnel/share data; do not merge it as advertising search-term performance.");
5515:   if (reportType === "TRANSACTION_REPORT") warnings.push("Combined Transaction Report is indexed by Posted Date. Taxes and transfers are excluded from product economics; advertising service fees are reconciliation-only.");
5516:   if (reportType === "ADS_REPORT") warnings.push(map.searchTerm ? "Metric grain=Search Term" : map.targeting ? "Metric grain=Targeting" : "Metric grain=Campaign; do not sum with another grain for the same period.");
5517:   return { schemaVersion: APP_SCHEMA_VERSION, fileName, reportType, adProduct: adProduct || "", attributionWindowDays, rowCount: rows.length || 0, headerCount: header.length || 0, missing, warnings, createdAt: new Date().toISOString() };
5518: };
5519: const recordSchemaAudit = (audit) => {
5520:   if (!audit) return;
5521:   AdsStore.schemaAudits.push(audit);
5522:   (audit.warnings || []).forEach(w => AdsStore.importWarnings.push({ fileName: audit.fileName, reportType: audit.reportType, warning: w }));
5523:   const label = audit.reportType === "ADS_REPORT" && audit.adProduct ? `${audit.reportType}/${getAdProductDisplayLabel(audit.adProduct)}` : audit.reportType;
5524:   if (audit.missing?.length) log(`Schema Audit ${label}: missing ${audit.missing.join(", ")}`, "warn");
5525:   else log(`Schema Audit ${label}: OK · rows=${audit.rowCount.toLocaleString()}${audit.attributionWindowDays ? ` · attribution=${audit.attributionWindowDays}d` : ""}`, "good");
5526:   (audit.warnings || []).forEach(w => log(`Guardrail: ${w}`, "warn"));
5527: };

5529: const normalizeAdProductValue = (value) => {
5530:     const v = String(value || "").trim().toLowerCase();
5531:     if (!v) return "";
5532:     if (v.includes("sponsored display") || v === "sd" || v.includes("display ads") || v.includes("display")) return "SD";
5533:     if (v.includes("sponsored brand") || v === "sb" || v.includes("brand")) return "SB";
5534:     if (v.includes("sponsored product") || v === "sp" || v.includes("product")) return "SP";
5535:     return "";
5536: };
5537: 
5538: const detectAdProduct = (headers, sampleRows = [], adProductCol = null) => {
5539:     if (adProductCol && sampleRows.length) {
5540:       for (const row of sampleRows.slice(0, 80)) {
5541:         const detected = normalizeAdProductValue(row?.[adProductCol]);
5542:         if (detected) return detected;
5543:       }
5544:     }
5545:     const joined = headers.map(cleanHeader).join("|");
5546:     if (joined.includes("viewableimpression") || joined.includes("vpm") || joined.includes("view-through") || joined.includes("viewthrough") || joined.includes("display")) return "SD";
5547:     if (joined.includes("ntb") || joined.includes("new-to-brand") || joined.includes("newtobrand") || joined.includes("brandimpression")) return "SB";
5548:     return "SP"; 
5549: };

5493:   if (/14(day|天)|14d/.test(joined)) return 14;

5529: const normalizeAdProductValue = (value) => {
5530:     const v = String(value || "").trim().toLowerCase();
5531:     if (!v) return "";
5532:     if (v.includes("sponsored display") || v === "sd" || v.includes("display ads") || v.includes("display")) return "SD";
5533:     if (v.includes("sponsored brand") || v === "sb" || v.includes("brand")) return "SB";
5534:     if (v.includes("sponsored product") || v === "sp" || v.includes("product")) return "SP";
5535:     return "";
5536: };
5537: 
5538: const detectAdProduct = (headers, sampleRows = [], adProductCol = null) => {
5539:     if (adProductCol && sampleRows.length) {
5540:       for (const row of sampleRows.slice(0, 80)) {
5541:         const detected = normalizeAdProductValue(row?.[adProductCol]);
5542:         if (detected) return detected;
5543:       }
5544:     }
5545:     const joined = headers.map(cleanHeader).join("|");
5546:     if (joined.includes("viewableimpression") || joined.includes("vpm") || joined.includes("view-through") || joined.includes("viewthrough") || joined.includes("display")) return "SD";
5547:     if (joined.includes("ntb") || joined.includes("new-to-brand") || joined.includes("newtobrand") || joined.includes("brandimpression")) return "SB";
5548:     return "SP"; 
5549: };

5487: const getAdProductMeta = (code) => AMAZON_AD_PRODUCT_META[String(code || "SP").toUpperCase()] || AMAZON_AD_PRODUCT_META.SP;
5488: const getAdProductDisplayLabel = (code) => getAdProductMeta(code).label;

5490: const isBulkAllowedAdProduct = (code) => Boolean(getAdProductMeta(code).bulkAllowed);
5491: const detectAttributionWindowFromHeader = (header = [], fallbackCode = "SP") => {
5492:   const joined = header.map(cleanHeaderCompact).join("|");
5493:   if (/14(day|天)|14d/.test(joined)) return 14;
5494:   if (/7(day|天)|7d/.test(joined)) return 7;
5495:   const advertiserType = $("advertiserType")?.value || "seller";
5496:   if (String(fallbackCode || "SP").toUpperCase() === "SP" && advertiserType === "vendor") return 14;
5497:   return getAdProductMeta(fallbackCode).defaultAttributionDays || 7;
5498: };
5499: const buildReportSchemaAudit = (reportType, header = [], map = {}, rows = [], fileName = "") => {
5500:   const warnings = [];
5501:   const requiredByType = {
5502:     ADS_REPORT: ["date", "campaign", "impr", "clicks", "spend", "sales7d", "orders7d"],
5503:     BUSINESS_REPORT: ["asin", "sessions", "units", "sales"],
5504:     PLACEMENT_REPORT: ["campaign", "placement", "impr", "clicks", "spend"],
5505:     SQP_REPORT: ["query", "searchVolume", "imprShare", "clickShare", "purchShare"],
5506:     TRANSACTION_REPORT: ["postedAt", "type", "productSales", "sellingFees", "fbaFees", "total", "status"]
5507:   };
5508:   const required = requiredByType[reportType] || [];
5509:   const missing = required.filter(k => !map[k]);
5510:   if (missing.length) warnings.push(`Missing columns: ${missing.join(", ")}`);
5511:   const adProduct = map.adProductType || (reportType === "ADS_REPORT" ? detectAdProduct(header, rows, map.adProduct) : "");
5512:   const attributionWindowDays = reportType === "ADS_REPORT" || reportType === "PLACEMENT_REPORT" ? detectAttributionWindowFromHeader(header, adProduct || "SP") : null;
5513:   if (reportType === "ADS_REPORT" && adProduct !== "SP") warnings.push(`${getAdProductDisplayLabel(adProduct)} imported as analysis-only; SP Bulk export is blocked for this report type.`);
5514:   if (reportType === "SQP_REPORT") warnings.push("SQP is search funnel/share data; do not merge it as advertising search-term performance.");
5515:   if (reportType === "TRANSACTION_REPORT") warnings.push("Combined Transaction Report is indexed by Posted Date. Taxes and transfers are excluded from product economics; advertising service fees are reconciliation-only.");
5516:   if (reportType === "ADS_REPORT") warnings.push(map.searchTerm ? "Metric grain=Search Term" : map.targeting ? "Metric grain=Targeting" : "Metric grain=Campaign; do not sum with another grain for the same period.");
5517:   return { schemaVersion: APP_SCHEMA_VERSION, fileName, reportType, adProduct: adProduct || "", attributionWindowDays, rowCount: rows.length || 0, headerCount: header.length || 0, missing, warnings, createdAt: new Date().toISOString() };
5518: };
5519: const recordSchemaAudit = (audit) => {
5520:   if (!audit) return;
5521:   AdsStore.schemaAudits.push(audit);
5522:   (audit.warnings || []).forEach(w => AdsStore.importWarnings.push({ fileName: audit.fileName, reportType: audit.reportType, warning: w }));
5523:   const label = audit.reportType === "ADS_REPORT" && audit.adProduct ? `${audit.reportType}/${getAdProductDisplayLabel(audit.adProduct)}` : audit.reportType;
5524:   if (audit.missing?.length) log(`Schema Audit ${label}: missing ${audit.missing.join(", ")}`, "warn");
5525:   else log(`Schema Audit ${label}: OK · rows=${audit.rowCount.toLocaleString()}${audit.attributionWindowDays ? ` · attribution=${audit.attributionWindowDays}d` : ""}`, "good");
5526:   (audit.warnings || []).forEach(w => log(`Guardrail: ${w}`, "warn"));
5527: };

5529: const normalizeAdProductValue = (value) => {
5530:     const v = String(value || "").trim().toLowerCase();
5531:     if (!v) return "";
5532:     if (v.includes("sponsored display") || v === "sd" || v.includes("display ads") || v.includes("display")) return "SD";
5533:     if (v.includes("sponsored brand") || v === "sb" || v.includes("brand")) return "SB";
5534:     if (v.includes("sponsored product") || v === "sp" || v.includes("product")) return "SP";
5535:     return "";
5536: };
5537: 
5538: const detectAdProduct = (headers, sampleRows = [], adProductCol = null) => {
5539:     if (adProductCol && sampleRows.length) {
5540:       for (const row of sampleRows.slice(0, 80)) {
5541:         const detected = normalizeAdProductValue(row?.[adProductCol]);
5542:         if (detected) return detected;
5543:       }
5544:     }
5545:     const joined = headers.map(cleanHeader).join("|");
5546:     if (joined.includes("viewableimpression") || joined.includes("vpm") || joined.includes("view-through") || joined.includes("viewthrough") || joined.includes("display")) return "SD";
5547:     if (joined.includes("ntb") || joined.includes("new-to-brand") || joined.includes("newtobrand") || joined.includes("brandimpression")) return "SB";
5548:     return "SP"; 
5549: };

5694: const normalizeRow = (raw, map, sourceFile) => {
5695:   if (!raw) return null; 
5696:   const impr = safeNum(raw[map.impr]);
5697:   const clicks = safeNum(raw[map.clicks]);
5698:   const spend = safeNum(raw[map.spend]); 
5699:   const sales = safeNum(raw[map.sales7d]);
5700:   const orders = safeNum(raw[map.orders7d]); 
5701:   const st = String(raw[map.searchTerm] ?? "").trim();
5702:   const acosVal = sales > 0 ? spend / sales : (spend > 0 ? Infinity : 0);
5703:   const rawAcos = map.acos ? parsePercent(raw[map.acos]) : acosVal;
5704:   const normalizedAcos = sales > 0 ? (rawAcos || acosVal) : (spend > 0 ? Infinity : 0);
5705:   const rawRoas = map.roas ? safeNum(raw[map.roas]) : (spend > 0 ? Math.max(0, sales) / spend : 0);
5706:   const normalizedRoas = spend > 0 ? Math.max(0, rawRoas || (sales / spend)) : 0;
5707: 
5708:   const adProduct = normalizeAdProductValue(map.adProduct ? raw[map.adProduct] : "") || map.adProductType || "SP";
5709:   const reportGranularity = map.searchTerm ? "searchTerm" : (map.targeting ? "targeting" : "campaign");
5710:   return {
5711:     sourceFile: intern(sourceFile), 
5712:     adProduct: intern(adProduct),
5713:     adProductLabel: intern(getAdProductDisplayLabel(adProduct)),
5714:     attributionWindowDays: map.attributionWindowDays || getAdProductMeta(adProduct).defaultAttributionDays || 7,
5715:     reportSchemaVersion: APP_SCHEMA_VERSION,
5716:     reportGranularity,
5717:     workspaceKey: intern(getWorkspaceKey()),
5718:     marketplace: intern(normalizeMarketplace(map.marketplace ? raw[map.marketplace] : getWorkspaceConfig().marketplace)),
5719:     accountName: intern(String(map.accountName ? raw[map.accountName] : getWorkspaceConfig().accountName).trim()),
5720:     date: intern(toISODate(raw[map.date])), 
5721:     portfolio: intern(String(raw[map.portfolio] ?? "").trim()), 
5722:     campaign: intern(String(raw[map.campaign] ?? "").trim()), 
5723:     adGroup: intern(String(raw[map.adGroup] ?? "").trim()), 
5724:     targeting: intern(String(raw[map.targeting] ?? "").trim()), 
5725:     matchType: intern(String(raw[map.matchType] ?? "").trim()), 
5726:     searchTerm: st, 
5727:     searchTermLower: st.toLowerCase(), 
5728:     searchTermRoot: searchTermToRoot(st),
5729:     advertisedAsin: intern(extractAsinFromText(map.advertisedAsin ? raw[map.advertisedAsin] : "") || ""),
5730:     advertisedSku: intern(String(map.advertisedSku ? raw[map.advertisedSku] : "").trim()),
5731:     purchasedAsin: intern(extractAsinFromText(map.purchasedAsin ? raw[map.purchasedAsin] : "") || ""),
5732:     purchasedSku: intern(String(map.purchasedSku ? raw[map.purchasedSku] : "").trim()),
5733:     advertisedSales: map.advertisedSales ? Math.max(0,safeNum(raw[map.advertisedSales])) : null,
5734:     advertisedUnits: map.advertisedUnits ? Math.max(0,safeNum(raw[map.advertisedUnits])) : null,
5735:     otherSkuSales: map.otherSkuSales ? Math.max(0,safeNum(raw[map.otherSkuSales])) : null,
5736:     otherSkuUnits: map.otherSkuUnits ? Math.max(0,safeNum(raw[map.otherSkuUnits])) : null,
5737:     currentBid: map.currentBid ? safeNum(raw[map.currentBid]) : null,
5738:     biddingStrategy: intern(String(map.biddingStrategy ? raw[map.biddingStrategy] : "").trim()),
5739:     topOfSearchAdjustment: map.topOfSearchAdjustment ? parsePercentField(raw[map.topOfSearchAdjustment],"placementAdjustment",sourceFile).value : null,
5740:     productPagesAdjustment: map.productPagesAdjustment ? parsePercentField(raw[map.productPagesAdjustment],"placementAdjustment",sourceFile).value : null,
5741:     restOfSearchAdjustment: map.restOfSearchAdjustment ? parsePercentField(raw[map.restOfSearchAdjustment],"placementAdjustment",sourceFile).value : null,
5742:     impr, clicks, spend, sales: Math.max(0, sales), orders,
5743:     units: map.units ? safeNum(raw[map.units]) : null,
5744:     ctr: map.ctr ? parsePercentField(raw[map.ctr],"ctr",sourceFile).value : (impr > 0 ? clicks / impr : 0), 
5745:     cpc: map.cpc ? safeNum(raw[map.cpc]) : (clicks > 0 ? spend / clicks : 0), 
5746:     cvr: map.cvr ? Math.min(1, parsePercentField(raw[map.cvr],"cvr",sourceFile).value) : (clicks > 0 ? Math.min(1, orders / clicks) : 0), 
5747:     acos: normalizedAcos, 
5748:     roas: normalizedRoas,
5749:   };
5750: };
5751: 
5752: const normalizeBrRow = (raw, map, sourceFile) => { 
5753:   const sessions = safeNum(raw[map.sessions]); 
5754:   const units = safeNum(raw[map.units]); 
5755:   const sales = safeNum(raw[map.sales]); 
5756:   const calculatedCvr = sessions > 0 ? Math.min(1, units / sessions) : 0; 
5757:   const calculatedAov = units > 0 ? sales / units : 0; 
5758:   return { 
5759:     sourceFile: intern(sourceFile), 
5760:     date: intern(map.date ? toISODate(raw[map.date]) : ""),
5761:     workspaceKey: intern(getWorkspaceKey()),
5762:     marketplace: intern(normalizeMarketplace(map.marketplace ? raw[map.marketplace] : getWorkspaceConfig().marketplace)),
5763:     asin: intern(String(raw[map.asin] ?? "").trim().toUpperCase()),
5764:     sku: intern(String(map.sku ? raw[map.sku] : "").trim()),
5765:     title: String(raw[map.title] ?? "").trim(), 
5766:     sessions, units, orders: map.orders ? safeNum(raw[map.orders]) : null, sales: Math.max(0, sales), 
5767:     cvr: isFinite(calculatedCvr) ? calculatedCvr : 0, 
5768:     aov: isFinite(calculatedAov) ? calculatedAov : 0 
5769:   }; 
5770: };
5771: 
5772: const normalizePlacementRow = (raw, map, sourceFile) => {
5773:     if (!raw) return null;

5833: const parseCSV = async file => {

5843:   }

5846: const XLSX_WORKER_LIB = "https://cdn.sheetjs.com/xlsx-0.20.3/package/dist/xlsx.full.min.js";
5847: const repairWorksheetRange = (ws) => {
5848:   if (!ws) return ws;
5849:   let maxR = -1, maxC = -1;
5850:   const dense = Array.isArray(ws) ? ws : (Array.isArray(ws["!data"]) ? ws["!data"] : null);
5851:   if (dense) {
5852:     for (let r = 0; r < dense.length; r++) {
5853:       const row = dense[r]; if (!row) continue;
5854:       for (let c = row.length - 1; c >= 0; c--) {
5855:         if (row[c] !== undefined && row[c] !== null) { maxR = Math.max(maxR, r); maxC = Math.max(maxC, c); break; }
5856:       }
5857:     }
5858:   } else {
5859:     for (const key of Object.keys(ws)) {
5860:       if (key[0] === "!") continue;
5861:       const m = /^([A-Z]+)(\d+)$/.exec(key); if (!m) continue;
5862:       let c = 0; for (const ch of m[1]) c = c * 26 + ch.charCodeAt(0) - 64;
5863:       maxR = Math.max(maxR, Number(m[2]) - 1); maxC = Math.max(maxC, c - 1);
5864:     }
5865:   }
5866:   if (maxR >= 0 && maxC >= 0) {
5867:     const actual = XLSX.utils.encode_range({s:{r:0,c:0},e:{r:maxR,c:maxC}});
5868:     const current = String(ws["!ref"] || "");
5869:     let currentRange = null; try { currentRange = current ? XLSX.utils.decode_range(current) : null; } catch (_) {}
5870:     if (!currentRange || currentRange.e.r < maxR || currentRange.e.c < maxC) ws["!ref"] = actual;
5871:   }
5872:   return ws;
5873: };
5874: const parseXLSXMainThread = async (buffer, maxRows) => {
5875:   const wb=XLSX.read(new Uint8Array(buffer),{type:"array",cellDates:false,dense:true});
5876:   if(wb.SheetNames.length>AMAZON_BULK_LIMITS.MAX_WORKSHEETS) throw new Error(`Workbook has ${wb.SheetNames.length} sheets; limit is ${AMAZON_BULK_LIMITS.MAX_WORKSHEETS}`);
5877:   const sheets=[]; let remaining=maxRows;
5878:   for(const sheetName of wb.SheetNames){
5879:     if(remaining<=0) break;
5880:     const ws=repairWorksheetRange(wb.Sheets[sheetName]);
5881:     let rows=XLSX.utils.sheet_to_json(ws,{defval:"",raw:true,blankrows:false});
5882:     if (!rows.length && ws && ws["!ref"] && ws["!ref"] !== "A1") {
5883:       rows=XLSX.utils.sheet_to_json(ws,{defval:"",raw:true,blankrows:false,range:ws["!ref"]});
5884:     }
5885:     const originalRows=rows.length; if(rows.length>remaining) rows=rows.slice(0,remaining);
5886:     rows.forEach(row=>{row.__sheetName=sheetName;});
5887:     if(rows.length){sheets.push({sheetName,rows,originalRows,truncated:originalRows>rows.length});remaining-=rows.length;}
5888:     await yieldToBrowser();
5889:   }
5890:   return sheets;
5891: };

5943:     const control = AdsStore.bidControlIndex.get(getBidControlKey(r));

5945:     if (!(Number.isFinite(r.currentBid) && r.currentBid > 0)) r.currentBid = control.currentBid;
5946:     if (!r.biddingStrategy) r.biddingStrategy = control.biddingStrategy;
5947:     if (!Number.isFinite(r.topOfSearchAdjustment)) r.topOfSearchAdjustment = control.topOfSearchAdjustment;
5948:     if (!Number.isFinite(r.productPagesAdjustment)) r.productPagesAdjustment = control.productPagesAdjustment;
5949:     if (!Number.isFinite(r.restOfSearchAdjustment)) r.restOfSearchAdjustment = control.restOfSearchAdjustment;
5950:     if (!r.advertisedAsin) r.advertisedAsin = control.advertisedAsin;
5951:     if (!r.advertisedSku) r.advertisedSku = control.advertisedSku;
5952:   }
5953: };
5954: const resolveAnalysisGrain = (rows = AdsStore.all, requested = "auto") => {
5955:   if (requested && requested !== "auto") return requested;
5956:   const stats=getGrainReconciliation(rows||[]),st=stats.searchTerm,tg=stats.targeting,cp=stats.campaign;
5957:   const score=x=>(x.spendCoverage||0)*.5+Math.min(1,(x.campaigns||0)/Math.max(1,Math.max(st.campaigns,tg.campaigns,cp.campaigns)))*.3+Math.min(1,(x.dates||0)/Math.max(1,Math.max(st.dates,tg.dates,cp.dates)))*.2;
5958:   if(st.rows&&score(st)>=score(tg)*.82)return "searchTerm";
5959:   if(tg.rows)return "targeting";
5960:   if(cp.rows)return "campaign";
5961:   return "searchTerm";
5962: };
5963: const weightedCoverage = (rows, predicate, weightKey = "spend") => {
5964:   let total=0, covered=0;
5965:   for (const r of rows || []) { const w=Math.max(0,safeNum(r[weightKey])) || (weightKey === "spend" ? Math.max(1,safeNum(r.clicks)) : 1); total+=w; if (predicate(r)) covered+=w; }
5966:   return total > 0 ? clamp(covered/total,0,1) : 0;
5967: };
5968: const getPeriodComparison = (rows = []) => {
5969:   const dates=[...new Set(rows.map(r=>r.date).filter(Boolean))].sort();
5970:   if (dates.length < 4) return null;
5971:   const window=Math.min(7,Math.floor(dates.length/2));
5972:   const recentDates=new Set(dates.slice(-window)), priorDates=new Set(dates.slice(-window*2,-window));
5973:   const recent=sumMetrics(rows.filter(r=>recentDates.has(r.date))), prior=sumMetrics(rows.filter(r=>priorDates.has(r.date)));
5974:   const delta=(a,b)=>b>0?(a-b)/b:(a>0?1:null);
5975:   return { window, recent, prior, spend:delta(recent.spend,prior.spend), sales:delta(recent.sales,prior.sales), roas:delta(recent.roas,prior.roas), cpc:delta(recent.cpc,prior.cpc), cvr:delta(recent.cvr,prior.cvr), profit:delta(recent.contributionProfit,prior.contributionProfit) };
5976: };
5977: const getDataQualityAudit = (rows = AdsStore.view || []) => {
5978:   const scope=getExecutiveDateScope(rows),total=sumMetrics(rows),now=new Date();now.setHours(0,0,0,0);const end=scope.end?new Date(scope.end+"T00:00:00"):null,staleDays=end?Math.max(0,Math.floor((now-end)/86400000)):999,dateCoverage=weightedCoverage(rows,r=>!!r.date,"spend"),structureCoverage=weightedCoverage(rows,r=>!!r.campaign&&!!r.adGroup,"spend"),asinCoverage=weightedCoverage(rows,r=>!!r.advertisedAsin,"spend"),bidCoverage=weightedCoverage(rows,r=>Number.isFinite(r.currentBid)&&r.currentBid>0,"spend"),strategyCoverage=weightedCoverage(rows,r=>!!r.biddingStrategy,"spend"),placementControlCoverage=weightedCoverage(rows,r=>Number.isFinite(r.topOfSearchAdjustment)||Number.isFinite(r.productPagesAdjustment)||Number.isFinite(r.restOfSearchAdjustment),"spend"),explicitUnitsCoverage=total.explicitUnitsCoverage??(total.units>0?clamp(total.explicitUnits/total.units,0,1):0),haloKnownCoverage=total.haloKnownCoverage??1,strictEconomicsCoverage=(explicitUnitsCoverage>=.90?0.5:0)+(haloKnownCoverage>=.90?0.5:0),metricAnomalyCount=(rows||[]).filter(r=>safeNum(r.clicks)>safeNum(r.impr)||(safeNum(r.clicks)<=0&&(safeNum(r.spend)>0||safeNum(r.orders)>0||safeNum(r.sales)>0))).length,metricAnomalyRate=(rows||[]).length?metricAnomalyCount/(rows||[]).length:0,econ=parseAsinEconomicsOverrides(),bizResult=getExecutiveBizSales(rows,scope),salesResult=getExecutiveAccountSales(rows,scope),adProducts=[...new 5979:   let sourceHealthScore=Math.round(clamp(dateCoverage*18+(1-Math.min(1,dupRate*5))*18+(1-Math.min(1,quarantineRate))*18+(workspaceMismatch?0:14)+(rawGrains.length?14:0)+(Math.max(recon.searchTerm.spendCoverage||0,recon.targeting.spendCoverage||0)>=.8?18:8)-Math.min(10,metricAnomalyRate*1000),0,100));

5986:   if(!negativeFreshEnough)alerts.push({level:"bad",text:`最新数据距今 ${staleDays} 天，超过否定/结构执行上限 ${negativeStaleLimit} 天；仅保留历史复核。`});else if(!bidFreshEnough)alerts.push({level:"warn",text:`最新数据距今 ${staleDays} 天：安全否定与结构候选可继续复核，但即时调价要求 ≤${bidStaleLimit} 天的新数据。`});

6897: const EVENT_ATTRIBUTION_RE = /\b(big\s*)?spring\s*sale\b|\bprime\s*day\b|\bblack\s*friday\b|\bcyber\s*monday\b|\bholiday\b|\bchristmas\b|\bpromo(?:tion)?\b|\bcoupon\b|\blightning\s*deal\b|\b7\s*day\s*deal\b|\bbest\s*deal\b|\bdeal\b|\bsale\b/i;

6928:   const dates = [...new Set(rows.map(r => r.date).filter(Boolean))].sort();
6929:   return { dates, days: dates.length, start: dates[0] || "", end: dates[dates.length - 1] || "" };

6932: const calcRecentSpendShare = (rows = [], item = {}, endDateStr = "", windowDays = 7) => {
6933:   const endDate = toDateOnly(endDateStr || getLatestDateFromRows(rows));
6934:   const totalSpend = safeNum(item.spend || rows.reduce((s, r) => s + safeNum(r.spend), 0));
6935:   if (!rows.length || !endDate || totalSpend <= 0) return 0;
6936:   const lookbackDays = Math.max(1, Math.min(7, windowDays));
6937:   const cutoff = new Date(endDate.getTime() - (lookbackDays - 1) * ATTRIBUTION_DAY_MS);
6938:   const recentSpend = rows.reduce((s, r) => {
6939:     const d = toDateOnly(r.date);
6940:     if (!d || d < cutoff || d > endDate) return s;
6941:     return s + safeNum(r.spend);
6942:   }, 0);
6943:   return clamp(recentSpend / totalSpend, 0, 1);
6944: };

6946: const getEventAttributionProfile = (item = {}) => {
6947:   const enabled = Boolean($("eventProtectionToggle")?.checked);
6948:   const rows = Array.isArray(item.rows) ? item.rows : [];
6949:   const adProducts = new Set();
6950:   if (item.adProduct) adProducts.add(item.adProduct);
6951:   if (Array.isArray(item.adProducts)) item.adProducts.forEach(x => adProducts.add(x));

6954:

6956:   const endDate = toDateOnly(endDateStr);
6957:   const today = new Date();

6959:   const todayUtc = new Date(Date.UTC(today.getFullYear(), today.getMonth(), today.getDate()));

6971:   const freshClickFallback = !eventSignal && daysSinceEnd <= 3 && recentSpendShare >= 0.70 && span.days <= Math.max(3, windowDays);

6985:     stageLabel = currentLang === "zh" ? "0-3天严格保护" : "0-3d strict guard";
6986:   } else if (watch) {

6989:     stageLabel = currentLang === "zh" ? "4-7天观察保护" : "4-7d attribution watch";
6990:   } else if (semiRelease) {

6993:     stageLabel = currentLang === "zh" ? "8-14天半释放" : "8-14d semi-release";
6994:   }

7014: const getDecisionConfidence = () => getNumericInput("decisionConfidence",0.90,0.50,0.99);
7015: const getMinStableDays = () => Math.round(getNumericInput("minStableDays",2,1,14));
7016: const getBayesianCvrStats = (item = {}, globalMetrics = null) => {
7017:   const g=globalMetrics||sumMetrics(AdsStore.view||[]), clicks=Math.max(0,safeNum(item.clicks)), orders=Math.max(0,Math.min(clicks,safeNum(item.orders)));
7018:   const priorMean=clamp(g.cvr||0.05,0.005,0.30), strength=24;
7019:   const a=priorMean*strength+orders, b=(1-priorMean)*strength+Math.max(0,clicks-orders), mean=a/(a+b);
7020:   const variance=(a*b)/(((a+b)**2)*(a+b+1)), sd=Math.sqrt(Math.max(0,variance));
7021:   const conf=getDecisionConfidence(), z=conf>=0.95?1.96:conf>=0.90?1.645:1.44;
7022:   const lower=clamp(mean-z*sd,0,1), upper=clamp(mean+z*sd,0,1);
7023:   const zeroOrderClicks=Math.ceil(Math.log(1-conf)/Math.log(Math.max(0.001,1-priorMean)));
7024:   return {priorMean,strength,mean,lower,upper,zeroOrderClicks,confidence:conf};
7025: };
7026: const getAdaptiveDecisionThresholds = (item = {}, targetAcos = null, globalMetrics = null) => {
7027:   const g=globalMetrics||sumMetrics(AdsStore.view||[]), stats=getBayesianCvrStats(item,g);
7028:   const aov=item.orders>0?item.sales/item.orders:(g.orders>0?g.sales/g.orders:15),targetReady=Number.isFinite(targetAcos)&&targetAcos>.005,targetCpa=targetReady?Math.max(1,aov*targetAcos):null,mismatch=getBidRiskProfile(item.name||item.searchTerm||item.targeting||"").hardMismatch;
7029:   const clickThreshold=Math.max(8,Math.ceil(stats.zeroOrderClicks*(mismatch?0.60:1.00)));
7030:   const spendThreshold=targetCpa!==null?Math.max(5,targetCpa*(mismatch?0.65:1.15)):0;
7031:   return {stats,aov,targetAcos:targetReady?targetAcos:null,targetReady,targetCpa,clickThreshold,spendThreshold};
7032: };

7037: const getBidGovernance = (item, rankBy, cachedGlobalMetrics = null) => {
7038:   const r = getRules();
7039:   const globalMetrics = cachedGlobalMetrics || sumMetrics(AdsStore.view);
7040:   const globalCvr = clamp(globalMetrics.cvr || 0.05, 0.005, 0.25);
7041:   const globalCpc = clamp(globalMetrics.cpc || 0.75, 0.15, 3.00);
7042:   const globalAov = globalMetrics.orders > 0 ? (globalMetrics.sales / globalMetrics.orders) : 20;
7043:   const aov = item.orders > 0 ? (item.sales / item.orders) : globalAov;
7044:   const targetPolicy=resolveUnifiedTargetPolicy({override:item.targetAcos,metrics:item,aov,asin:item.advertisedAsin||""}),targetAcos=targetPolicy.value,economicsReady=targetPolicy.ready;
